Go into the bank, find out which company the payment came from, then match it to the correct invoice manually. • The software can be unreliable. Watch out for duplicates — this is crucial. For example, if a client has two unpaid invoices but only pays one, and the software duplicates that transaction, it might look like both invoices were paid. That would make us lose one payment without even realizing it. That’s why the bank is always the final authority. The spreadsheet must calculate and minimize tax liability when gradually moving funds from General Investment Accounts (GIAs) and savings accounts into ISAs (Individual Savings Account) over successive tax years, accounting for dividend income, capital gains, and various tax allowances. KEY REQUIREMENTS 1. VARIABLE INPUTS (User-Configurable) The spreadsheet must allow users to input the following variables: Legislative Variables: • Maximum Tax-Free Lump Sum allowed (currently £268,275) • Dividend Allowance per person (currently £500 per person = £1,000 for couple) • Capital Gains Tax Allowance per person (currently £3,000 per person = £6,000 for couple) • ISA Allowance per person per tax year (currently £20,000 per person = £40,000 for couple) • Basic rate Dividend Tax rate (currently 8.75%) • Basic rate Capital Gains Tax rate (currently 10%) Maximum interest that can be earned in a savings account is £1000 per individual Investment Return Variables: • Annual return on GIA investments (% per annum - split between capital growth % and dividend yield %) • Annual interest rate on savings accounts (% per annum) Strategy Variables: • Amount allocated to GIA vs savings accounts from the initial lump sum • Amount to transfer to ISAs each tax year per person 2. CALCULATION REQUIREMENTS The spreadsheet must calculate for each tax year (Tax Year 1, Tax Year 2, Tax Year 3, etc.) until the entire tax-free lump sum is sheltered in ISAs: For GIA Holdings: • Opening balance • Capital growth during year • Dividend income during year • Amount transferred to ISAs (at start of tax year) • Closing balance • Taxable dividends (after allowances) • Taxable capital gains (after allowances) • Dividend tax payable • Capital Gains Tax payable • Total tax for the year For Savings Account Holdings: • Opening balance • Interest earned during year • Amount transferred to ISAs (if applicable) • Closing balance • Taxable interest (after Personal Savings Allowance - £1,000 per person for basic rate taxpayers) • Tax on interest payable For ISA Holdings: • Opening balance • Contributions during year • Growth during year (tax-free) • Closing balance Summary Outputs: • Total tax paid each year • Cumulative tax paid • Total amount sheltered in ISAs to date • Amount remaining in taxable accounts • Year when full lump sum is ISA-sheltered • Total tax paid over entire period 3. OPTIMIZATION FEATURES The spreadsheet should help users minimize tax by: • Clearly showing tax liability each year • Allowing users to model different transfer strategies (e.g., transferring more/less each year) • Highlighting when allowances are fully utilized vs when they're being wasted • Comparing different allocation strategies (e.g., GIA vs savings account split) 4. FUNCTIONALITY REQUIREMENTS • Professional formatting with clear sections and labels • Input validation to prevent errors • Clear instructions for users • Summary dashboard showing key metrics • Ability to easily adjust variables and see updated calculations • Cells should be appropriately locked/unlocked (inputs unlocked, calculations locked) • Include notes/comments explaining key assumptions 5. TECHNICAL REQUIREMENTS • No macros or VBA required - pure formula-based • Must be robust and error-free • Should handle edge cases (e.g., lump sum fully sheltered before all allowances used) CURRENT UK TAX RULES (2025/26) TO BE USED AS DEFAULTS • Maximum Tax-Free Lump Sum: £268,275 • ISA Allowance: £20,000 per person per tax year • Dividend Allowance: £500 per person per tax year • Capital Gains Tax Allowance: £3,000 per person per tax year • Basic Rate Dividend Tax: 8.75% • Basic Rate Capital Gains Tax: 10% • Personal Savings Allowance (basic rate): £1,000 per person per tax year DELIVERABLES 1. Completed spreadsheet (Google Sheets format) 2. Brief user guide (can be embedded in spreadsheet) 3. Example scenario populated with sample data 4. Source file with formulas visible for verification IDEAL CANDIDATE • Proven experience creating complex financial/tax calculators in Excel/Google Sheets • Strong understanding of UK tax system (particularly ISAs, CGT, dividend tax) • Excellent formula skills (INDEX, MATCH, SUMIFS, etc.) • Attention to detail and ability to handle edge cases • Clear documentation skills • Portfolio of similar work preferred PROJECT TIMELINE • Deadline: 3 days from start date. • Revisions: Up to 2 rounds of revisions included HOW TO APPLY Please provide: 1. Your project quote 2. Estimated timeline for completion 3. Links to similar spreadsheet projects you've completed 4. Brief description of your approach to this project 5.
